<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">before, in front</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:staan.html>staan</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to stand</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***voorstellen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:voorstellen.html>voorstellen</a> (884)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">vorestellen</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stellen.html>stellen</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:voorstellen.html>voorstellen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to present, to put forth, to introduce</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to propose, to suggest
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:schaal.html>Schaal</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> Kardasjev <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:russische.html>Russische</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:astronoom.html>astronoom</a> Nikolaj Kardasjev <b>voorgestelde</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:indeling.html>indeling</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:technologische.html>technologische</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ontwikkeling.html>ontwikkeling</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:beschavingen.html>beschavingen</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The Kardashev scale <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a system <b>proposed</b> by the Russian astronomer Nicolai Kardashev for classifying the technological development of civilizations.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">reflexive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to imagine
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:stel.html>Stel</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geen.html>geen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:landen.html>landen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>Imagine</b> there's no countries.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to amount to, to matter, to be important
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dacht.html>dacht</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eerst.html>eerst</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zoveel.html>zoveel</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:voorstelde.html>voorstelde</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I thought at first that it didn'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> <b>matter</b> too much.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to represent, to depict
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> Egyptische <a href = vnd.unilang:goden.html>goden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:werden.html>werden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mensen.html>mensen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> dierenhoofden <b><a href = vnd.unilang:voorgesteld.html>voorgesteld</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The Egyptian <a href = vnd.unilang:gods.html>gods</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> <b>represented</b> as humans with animal heads.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:vort.html>vort</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:voort.html>voort</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">forth</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*furþa-</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*pr̥to-</i>. ***vor.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vor.html>vor</a> (58640)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <small>[Term?]</small>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">fora</i>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*per-</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a></i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">fore</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Preposition_2">Preposition</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:vor.html>vor</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">before</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">prior to</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">ahead of</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">time</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="de">bevor</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">ahead of</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">in front of</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">space</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">ago</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">time</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="de"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:vor.html>vor</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:drei.html>drei</a> Tagen</i> ― <span class="e-translation">three days <b>ago</b></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="de"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:vor.html>vor</a></b> einiger Zeit</i> ― <span class="e-translation">a while <b>ago</b></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>from, against <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">when involving protecting, hiding, escaping, rescuing/saving</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">because of</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">for</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">in select phrases</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:wegen.html>wegen</a></span></span></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="de"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:vor.html>vor</a></b> Freude <a href = vnd.unilang:springen.html>springen</a></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to jump <b>for</b> joy</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The preposition <i><a href = vnd.unilang:vor.html>vor</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used with accusative case if the verb <a href = vnd.unilang:shows.html>shows</a> movement from one place to another, whereas it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used with dative case if the verb <a href = vnd.unilang:shows.html>shows</a> location.
</p>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:vormen.html>vorme</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">forme</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:forma.html>forma</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">shape, figure, image, outline, plan, mold, frame, case, etc., manner, sort, <a href = vnd.unilang:kind.html>kind</a>, etc.</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***vormen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vormen.html>vormen</a> (2293)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:vormen.html>vormen</a></i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vorm.html>vorm</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vormen.html>vormen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to form, mold</li>
<li>to make up, constitute</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">vermen</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:vormen.html>vormen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">firmō</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vormen.html>vormen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">Christianity</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to confirm an already baptised Christian</li></ol>

***vorst.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vorst.html>vorst</a> (8776)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:vorst.html>vorst</a></i>, a metathetic form of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*frost</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*frustaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vorst.html>vorst</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>frost, freeze, <a href = vnd.unilang:frosty.html>frosty</a> weather</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:vorsen.html>vorste</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">furista</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">fursta</i>, from the substantivised weak inflection of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*furistaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">first</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vorst.html>vorst</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vorsten.html>vorsten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vorst.html>vorstje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vorstin.html>vorstin</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>generic term for prince, monarch, ruler</li>
<li>prince, rendering of tradition-specific title of certain <a href = vnd.unilang:ranks.html>ranks</a> (all below King)</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:prins.html>prins</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:vorst.html>vorst</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">voerst</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">furost</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*furhiþą</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vorst.html>vorst</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vorsten.html>vorsten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vorst.html>vorstje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>wood(<a href = vnd.unilang:land.html>land</a>), forest</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology 4</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:vorst.html>vorst</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:vorsen.html>vorste</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*furstiz</i>, variant of <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*firstiz</i>. Most closely related to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml"><a href = vnd.unilang:vorst.html>vorst</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">forst</i>. Through the <i>i</i>-form also cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:verst.html>verst</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:verste.html>verste</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">faîte</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">First</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">first</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vorstin.html>vorstin</a> (31475)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">vorstinne</i>. </p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vorstin.html>vorstin</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vorstinnen.html>vorstinnen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vorstin.html>vorstinnetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>, <i>masculine</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vorst.html>vorst</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>a princess, the daughter of a king, elector (in the Holy Roman Empire), emperor, or the wife or daughter of certain <a href = vnd.unilang:princes.html>princes</a></li>
<li>a princess, the female reigning monarch of a principality</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">generic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a female potentate, such as certain especially mediaeval duchesses</li></ol>

***vos.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vos.html>vos</a> (5791)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:vos.html>vos</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">fus</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">vus</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*fuhsaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vos.html>vos</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vossen.html>vossen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vosje.html>vosje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">vossin</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>fox, carnivore of the tribe Vulpini</li>
<li>red fox specifically, <i>Vulpes vulpes</i>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gewone.html>gewone</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vos.html>vos</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rode.html>rode</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vos.html>vos</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>fox fur</li>
<li>a crafty, ingenious person
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:koen.html>Koen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lepe.html>lepe</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:vos.html>vos</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:laat.html>laat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zich.html>zich</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:luren.html>luren</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:leggen.html>leggen</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Conrad <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a sly <b>fox</b> who does not allow himself to be hoodwinked.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>horse with red or red-brown fur</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>See the etymology of the main entry.
</p>

</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:dierkunde.html>dierkunde</a>)</span> <i>Vulpes vulpes</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:roofdier.html>roofdier</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> bruinrode <a href = vnd.unilang:kleur.html>kleur</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> dikbehaarde <a href = vnd.unilang:staart.html>staart</a>.
<dl><dd><ul><li><i>In <a href = vnd.unilang:dit.html>dit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gebied.html>gebied</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:vossen.html>vossen</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:losgelaten.html>losgelaten</a>.</i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li>
<li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:scheikunde.html>scheikunde</a>)</span> <span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:afkorting.html>afkorting</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:afkorting.html>afkorting</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> '<a href = vnd.unilang:vluchtig.html>Vluchtige</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:organische.html>organische</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stof.html>stof</a>' -gt; dichloorvos</li>
<li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:afkorting.html>afkorting</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:afkorting.html>afkorting</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> '<a href = vnd.unilang:vrouwen.html>Vrouwen</a> oriënteren <a href = vnd.unilang:zich.html>zich</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:samenleving.html>samenleving</a>' -gt; voscursus</li>
<li><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bont.html>bont</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vos.html>vos</a>.</li>
